 1 | const fs = require('node:fs');
 2 | const path = require('node:path');
 3 | 
 4 | const projectRoot = path.resolve(__dirname, '..');
 5 | const sourceServerDir = path.join(projectRoot, 'server');
 6 | const distDir = path.join(projectRoot, 'dist');
 7 | const distServerDir = path.join(distDir, 'server');
 8 | 
 9 | function ensureFrontendBuildExists() {
10 |   const indexHtmlPath = path.join(distDir, 'index.html');
11 |   if (!fs.existsSync(indexHtmlPath)) {
12 |     throw new Error('Frontend bundle is missing. Run `vite build` first.');
13 |   }
14 | }
15 | 
16 | function copyServerFiles() {
17 |   const serverFiles = fs
18 |     .readdirSync(sourceServerDir, { withFileTypes: true })
19 |     .filter((entry) => entry.isFile() && entry.name.endsWith('.cjs'))
20 |     .map((entry) => entry.name);
21 | 
22 |   fs.rmSync(distServerDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
23 |   fs.mkdirSync(distServerDir, { recursive: true });
24 | 
25 |   for (const fileName of serverFiles) {
26 |     const sourcePath = path.join(sourceServerDir, fileName);
27 |     const targetPath = path.join(distServerDir, fileName);
28 |     fs.copyFileSync(sourcePath, targetPath);
29 |   }
30 | 
31 |   return serverFiles;
32 | }
33 | 
34 | function buildServerBundle() {
35 |   ensureFrontendBuildExists();
36 |   const copiedFiles = copyServerFiles();
37 |   console.log(`Bundled backend files: ${copiedFiles.join(', ')}`);
38 |   console.log(`Output directory: ${path.relative(projectRoot, distServerDir)}`);
39 | }
40 | 
41 | buildServerBundle();

 4 | const cors = require('cors');
 5 | const { makePDF } = require('./pdfMaker.cjs');
 6 | 
 7 | const app = express();
 8 | const port = Number(process.env.PORT || 8787);
 9 | 
10 | app.use(cors());
11 | app.use(express.json({ limit: '25mb' }));
12 | 
13 | app.get('/api/health', (_req, res) => {
14 |   res.json({ ok: true });
15 | });
16 | 
17 | app.post('/api/generate-pdf', async (req, res) => {
18 |   try {
19 |     const pdfBytes = await makePDF(req.body || {});
20 |     res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/pdf');
21 |     res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename="merged.pdf"');
22 |     res.send(Buffer.from(pdfBytes));
23 |   } catch (error) {
24 |     console.error('PDF generation failed:', error);
25 |     res.status(500).json({
26 |       success: false,
27 |       message: error.message || 'Failed to generate PDF',
28 |     });
29 |   }
30 | });
31 | 
32 | const frontendCandidates = [
33 |   path.resolve(__dirname, '..', 'dist'),
34 |   path.resolve(__dirname, '..'),
35 | ];
36 | 
37 | const frontendDir = frontendCandidates.find((candidate) =>
38 |   fs.existsSync(path.join(candidate, 'index.html')),
39 | );
40 | 
41 | if (frontendDir) {
42 |   app.use(express.static(frontendDir));
43 |   app.get(/^\/(?!api).*/, (_req, res) => {
44 |     res.sendFile(path.join(frontendDir, 'index.html'));
45 |   });
46 | }
47 | 
48 | app.listen(port, () => {
49 |   console.log(`PDF API listening on http://localhost:${port}`);

 21 | function getEmailWidth(emailType, shamanMode, breakpointWidth) {
 22 |   if (shamanMode === 'shaman_mass') return 730;
 23 |   if (shamanMode === 'shaman_veeva') return 730;
 24 |   if (emailType !== 'mass' && breakpointWidth === 599) return 610;
 25 |   return emailType === 'mass' ? 710 : 710;
 26 | }
 27 | 
 28 | function detectBreakpointWidth(html) {
 29 |   if (/max-width:\s*599px/i.test(html)) return 599;
 30 |   if (/max-width:\s*699px/i.test(html)) return 699;
 31 |   return null;
 32 | }
 33 | 
 34 | function escapeRegExp(value) {
 35 |   return value.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
 36 | }
 37 | 
 38 | function escapeHtml(value) {
 39 |   return value
 40 |     .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
 41 |     .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
 42 |     .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
 43 |     .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
 44 |     .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
 45 | }

 47 | function getDocumentDimensions(page) {
 48 |   return page.evaluate(() => {
 49 |     const body = document.body;
 50 |     const html = document.documentElement;
 51 |     return {
 52 |       width: Math.max(
 53 |         body.scrollWidth,
 54 |         body.offsetWidth,
 55 |         html.clientWidth,
 56 |         html.scrollWidth,
 57 |         html.offsetWidth,
 58 |       ),
 59 |       height: Math.max(
 60 |         body.scrollHeight,
 61 |         body.offsetHeight,
 62 |         html.clientHeight,
 63 |         html.scrollHeight,
 64 |         html.offsetHeight,
 65 |       ),
 66 |     };
 67 |   });
 68 | }

 70 | async function waitForPageAssets(page, timeoutMs = 20000) {
 71 |   const imagesLoaded = page.evaluate(async () => {
 72 |     const imageElements = Array.from(document.images || []);
 73 |     if (!imageElements.length) return;
 74 | 
 75 |     await Promise.all(
 76 |       imageElements.map((imageElement) => {
 77 |         if (imageElement.complete) return Promise.resolve();
 78 |         return new Promise((resolve) => {
 79 |           imageElement.addEventListener('load', resolve, { once: true });
 80 |           imageElement.addEventListener('error', resolve, { once: true });
 81 |         });
 82 |       }),
 83 |     );
 84 |   });
 85 | 
 86 |   await Promise.all([
 87 |     Promise.race([
 88 |       imagesLoaded,
 89 |       new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, timeoutMs)),
 90 |     ]),
 91 |     page.waitForNetworkIdle({ idleTime: 500, timeout: timeoutMs }).catch(() => {}),
 92 |   ]);
 93 | }
 94 | 
 95 | function extractGifSrcs(htmlString) {
 96 |   const $ = cheerio.load(htmlString);
 97 |   const srcList = [];
 98 | 
 99 |   $('img').each((index, element) => {
100 |     const src = $(element).attr('src');
101 |     if (!src) return;
102 | 
103 |     const srcLower = src.toLowerCase();
104 |     if (src === 'https://a-cf65.gskstatic.com/etc/designs/default/0.gif') return;
105 |     if (srcLower.endsWith('.gif') || srcLower.startsWith('data:image/gif;base64')) {
106 |       srcList.push(src);
107 |     }
108 |   });
109 | 
110 |   return srcList;
111 | }
112 | 
113 | function downloadFile(url, destinationPath, redirectCount = 0) {
114 |   if (redirectCount > 5) {
115 |     return Promise.reject(new Error('Too many redirects while downloading GIF.'));
116 |   }
117 | 
118 |   const client = url.startsWith('https://') ? https : http;
119 | 
120 |   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
121 |     const request = client.get(url, (response) => {
122 |       const statusCode = response.statusCode || 0;
123 | 
124 |       if (statusCode >= 300 && statusCode < 400 && response.headers.location) {
125 |         const redirectUrl = new URL(response.headers.location, url).toString();
126 |         response.destroy();
127 |         downloadFile(redirectUrl, destinationPath, redirectCount + 1).then(resolve).catch(reject);
128 |         return;
129 |       }
130 | 
131 |       if (statusCode >= 400) {
132 |         reject(new Error(`Failed to download GIF: HTTP ${statusCode}`));
133 |         return;
134 |       }
135 | 
136 |       const file = fs.createWriteStream(destinationPath);
137 |       response.pipe(file);
138 |       file.on('finish', () => {
139 |         file.close(resolve);
140 |       });
141 |       file.on('error', reject);
142 |     });
143 | 
144 |     request.on('error', reject);
145 |   });
146 | }
147 | 
148 | async function extractGifFrameAsBase64(input, timestamp = 1.5) {
149 |   if (!ffmpegPath) {
150 |     throw new Error('ffmpeg binary not found.');
151 |   }
152 | 
153 |   const tempRoot = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'pdf-maker-gif-'));
154 |   const gifPath = path.join(tempRoot, `${randomUUID()}.gif`);
155 |   const framePath = path.join(tempRoot, `${randomUUID()}.png`);
156 | 
157 |   try {
158 |     if (input.startsWith('data:')) {
159 |       const base64Data = input.split(',')[1] || '';
160 |       await fs.promises.writeFile(gifPath, Buffer.from(base64Data, 'base64'));
161 |     } else if (input.startsWith('http://') || input.startsWith('https://')) {
162 |       await downloadFile(input, gifPath);
163 |     } else {
164 |       throw new Error('Invalid GIF input source.');
165 |     }
166 | 
167 |     await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
168 |       ffmpeg(gifPath)
169 |         .screenshots({
170 |           timestamps: [String(timestamp)],
171 |           filename: path.basename(framePath),
172 |           folder: tempRoot,
173 |           size: '500x?',
174 |         })
175 |         .on('end', resolve)
176 |         .on('error', reject);
177 |     });
178 | 
179 |     const imageData = await fs.promises.readFile(framePath);
180 |     return `data:image/png;base64,${imageData.toString('base64')}`;
181 |   } finally {
182 |     await fs.promises.rm(tempRoot, { recursive: true, force: true });
183 |   }
184 | }
185 | 
186 | function buildAltTextHtml(htmlContent) {
187 |   const dom = new JSDOM(htmlContent);
188 |   const document = dom.window.document;
189 |   const imgElements = document.querySelectorAll('img');
190 | 
191 |   imgElements.forEach((imgElement) => {
192 |     const parentElement = imgElement.parentNode;
193 | 
194 |     if (parentElement && parentElement.nodeType === 1) {
195 |       const existingStyles = parentElement.getAttribute('style') || '';
196 |       const updatedStyles = `${existingStyles};font-size: 14px;`;
197 |       parentElement.setAttribute('style', updatedStyles);
198 |     }
199 | 
200 |     imgElement.style.fontStyle = 'italic';
201 |     imgElement.style.overflow = 'visible';
202 |     imgElement.style.lineHeight = '14px';
203 | 
204 |     if (imgElement.getAttribute('alt') === 'Trans icon') {
205 |       imgElement.alt = '';
206 |     }
207 | 
208 |     const widthAttr = Number(imgElement.getAttribute('width') || 0);
209 |     if (widthAttr && widthAttr <= 45) {
210 |       if (!imgElement.getAttribute('alt')) {
211 |         imgElement.alt = '.';
212 |         imgElement.style.fontSize = '0px';
213 |       } else {
214 |         const adjustedWidth = (imgElement.getAttribute('alt').length || 0) * 12;
215 |         imgElement.width = adjustedWidth > 80 ? 80 : adjustedWidth;
216 |       }
217 |     }
218 |   });
219 | 
220 |   const updatedHtml = dom.serialize();
221 |   return updatedHtml.replace(/src/g, 'srt');
222 | }
223 | 
224 | function buildSummaryHtml(htmlContent, subjectLines, preheaderLines) {
225 |   const $ = cheerio.load(htmlContent);
226 |   const finalSubjects = [...subjectLines];
227 |   const finalPreheaders = [...preheaderLines];
228 | 
229 |   const title = $('title').text().trim();
230 |   if (title) {
231 |     finalSubjects.unshift(title);
232 |   }
233 | 
234 |   let preheader = $('body > div:first').text().trim();
235 |   if ($('body > div:first').attr('id') === 'canvas' || preheader === '') {
236 |     preheader = null;
237 |   }
238 |   if (preheader) {
239 |     finalPreheaders.unshift(preheader);
240 |   }
241 | 
242 |   const subjectMarkup = finalSubjects
243 |     .map((line, index) => {
244 |       const label = finalSubjects.length === 1 ? 'Subject Line:' : `Subject Line ${index + 1}:`;
245 |       return `
246 |         <div style="text-align:left;padding-top:6px;">
247 |           <strong style="font-size:16px;line-height:24px;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">${label} </strong>
248 |           <span style="font-size:16px;line-height:24px;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">${escapeHtml(line)}</span>
249 |         </div>
250 |       `;
251 |     })
252 |     .join('');
253 | 
254 |   const preheaderMarkup = finalPreheaders
255 |     .map((line, index) => {
256 |       const label = finalPreheaders.length === 1 ? 'PreHeader:' : `PreHeader ${index + 1}:`;
257 |       return `
258 |         <div style="text-align:left;padding-top:6px;">
259 |           <strong style="font-size:16px;line-height:24px;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">${label} </strong>
260 |           <span style="font-size:16px;line-height:24px;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">${escapeHtml(line)}</span>
261 |         </div>
262 |       `;
263 |     })
264 |     .join('');
265 | 
266 |   return `
267 |     <html lang="en">
268 |       <head>
269 |         <meta charset="UTF-8" />
270 |         <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
271 |       </head>
272 |       <body style="margin:0;padding:20px 10px 20px 10px;">
273 |         ${subjectMarkup}
274 |         ${preheaderMarkup}
275 |       </body>
276 |     </html>
277 |   `;
278 | }

280 | function resolveExecutablePath() {
281 |   const configured = process.env.PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH;
282 |   if (configured && fs.existsSync(configured)) return configured;
283 |   if (fs.existsSync(DEFAULT_CHROME_PATH)) return DEFAULT_CHROME_PATH;
284 |   return null;
285 | }

287 | async function launchBrowser() {
288 |   const launchOptions = {
289 |     headless: 'new',
290 |     timeout: 80000,
291 |   };
292 |

294 |   if (executablePath) {
295 |     launchOptions.executablePath = executablePath;
296 |   }

301 | async function makePDF(requestBody) {
302 |   if (!requestBody || typeof requestBody.data !== 'string') {
303 |     throw new Error('Invalid payload: `data` (email HTML) is required.');
304 |   }
305 | 
306 |   const inputHtml = requestBody.data.replace(/%%\[[\s\S]*?\]%%/g, '');
307 |   if (!inputHtml.trim()) {
308 |     throw new Error('Email HTML cannot be empty.');
309 |   }
310 | 
311 |   const emailType = inputHtml.includes('%%=ContentBlockByKey') ? 'mass' : 'veeva';
312 |   const subjectLines = String(requestBody.subject2 || '')
313 |     .split('\n')
314 |     .map((value) => value.trim())
315 |     .filter(Boolean);
316 |   const preheaderLines = String(requestBody.preheader2 || '')
317 |     .split('\n')
318 |     .map((value) => value.trim())
319 |     .filter(Boolean);
320 |   const includeMobileView = Boolean(requestBody.mobileView);
321 | 
322 |   let shamanMode = requestBody.shaman ? 'shaman' : '';
323 |   if (shamanMode && inputHtml.includes('@media (max-width: 720px)')) {
324 |     shamanMode = 'shaman_mass';
325 |   } else if (shamanMode && inputHtml.includes('@media (max-width: 620px)')) {
326 |     shamanMode = 'shaman_veeva';
327 |   }
328 | 
329 |   const breakpointWidth = detectBreakpointWidth(inputHtml);
330 |   const widthValue = getEmailWidth(emailType, shamanMode, breakpointWidth);
331 |   let htmlForRendering = inputHtml;
332 | 
333 |   const gifSources = extractGifSrcs(htmlForRendering);
334 |   for (const gifUrl of gifSources) {
335 |     if (!htmlForRendering.includes(gifUrl)) continue; 
336 | 
337 |     try {
338 |       const gifFrame = await extractGifFrameAsBase64(gifUrl);
339 |       const gifRegex = new RegExp(escapeRegExp(gifUrl), 'g');
340 |       htmlForRendering = htmlForRendering.replace(gifRegex, gifFrame);
341 |     } catch (error) {
342 |       console.warn(`GIF replacement skipped for ${gifUrl}:`, error.message);
343 |     }
344 |   }
345 | 
346 |   const browser = await launchBrowser();
347 | 
348 |   try {
349 |     const firstPage = await browser.newPage();
350 |     await firstPage.setCacheEnabled(false);
351 |     await firstPage.setViewport({
352 |       width: widthValue,
353 |       height: 600,
354 |       isMobile: true,
355 |       deviceScaleFactor: 1,
356 |     });
357 |     await firstPage.setContent(htmlForRendering, {
358 |       waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded',
359 |       timeout: 30000,
360 |     });
361 |     await firstPage.emulateMediaType('screen');
362 |     await waitForPageAssets(firstPage);
363 | 
364 |     const firstPageDimensions = await getDocumentDimensions(firstPage);
365 |     const pdf1Buffer = await firstPage.pdf({
366 |       width: `${firstPageDimensions.width + 20}px`,
367 |       height: `${firstPageDimensions.height + 20}px`,
368 |       printBackground: true,
369 |       scale: 1,
370 |       margin: { top: '10px', right: '10px', bottom: '10px', left: '10px' },
371 |     });
372 |     await firstPage.close();
373 | 
374 |     let pdfMobileBuffer = null;
375 |     if (includeMobileView) {
376 |       const mobilePage = await browser.newPage();
377 |       await mobilePage.setCacheEnabled(false);
378 |       await mobilePage.emulate(MOBILE_DEVICE);
379 |       await mobilePage.setViewport({
380 |         width: 420,
381 |         height: 500,
382 |         isMobile: true,
383 |         deviceScaleFactor: 2,
384 |       });
385 |       await mobilePage.setContent(htmlForRendering, {
386 |         waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded',
387 |         timeout: 30000,
388 |       });
389 |       await mobilePage.emulateMediaType('screen');
390 |       await waitForPageAssets(mobilePage);
391 | 
392 |       const screenshot = await mobilePage.screenshot({
393 |         type: 'png',
394 |         fullPage: true,
395 |         omitBackground: false,
396 |       });
397 |       await mobilePage.close();
398 | 
399 |       const MOBILE_SIDE_MARGIN = 10;
400 |       const mobileDoc = await PDFDocument.create();
401 |       const mobileImage = await mobileDoc.embedPng(screenshot);
402 |       const mobilePageWidth = mobileImage.width + MOBILE_SIDE_MARGIN * 2;
403 |       const mobileImagePage = mobileDoc.addPage([mobilePageWidth, mobileImage.height]);
404 |       mobileImagePage.drawRectangle({
405 |         x: 0,
406 |         y: 0,
407 |         width: mobilePageWidth,
408 |         height: mobileImage.height,
409 |         color: rgb(1, 1, 1),
410 |       });
411 |       mobileImagePage.drawImage(mobileImage, {
412 |         x: MOBILE_SIDE_MARGIN,
413 |         y: 0,
414 |         width: mobileImage.width,
415 |         height: mobileImage.height,
416 |       });
417 |       pdfMobileBuffer = await mobileDoc.save();
418 |     }
419 | 
420 |     const altHtml = buildAltTextHtml(htmlForRendering);
421 |     const secondPage = await browser.newPage();
422 |     await secondPage.setCacheEnabled(false);
423 |     await secondPage.setViewport({
424 |       width: widthValue,
425 |       height: 600,
426 |       isMobile: true,
427 |       deviceScaleFactor: 1,
428 |     });
429 |     await secondPage.setContent(altHtml, {
430 |       waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded',
431 |       timeout: 30000,
432 |     });
433 |     await secondPage.emulateMediaType('screen');
434 |     await waitForPageAssets(secondPage);
435 | 
436 |     const secondPageDimensions = await getDocumentDimensions(secondPage);
437 |     const pdf2Buffer = await secondPage.pdf({
438 |       width: `${firstPageDimensions.width + 20}px`,
439 |       height: `${secondPageDimensions.height + 20}px`,
440 |       printBackground: true,
441 |       scale: 1,
442 |       margin: { top: '10px', right: '10px', bottom: '10px', left: '10px' },
443 |     });
444 |     await secondPage.close();
445 | 
446 |     const summaryHtml = buildSummaryHtml(htmlForRendering, subjectLines, preheaderLines);
447 |     const summaryPage = await browser.newPage();
448 |     await summaryPage.setCacheEnabled(false);
449 |     await summaryPage.setViewport({
450 |       width: widthValue,
451 |       height: 200,
452 |       deviceScaleFactor: 1,
453 |     });
454 |     await summaryPage.setContent(summaryHtml, {
455 |       waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded',
456 |       timeout: 30000,
457 |     });
458 |     await summaryPage.emulateMediaType('screen');
459 |     await waitForPageAssets(summaryPage);
460 | 
461 |     const summaryDimensions = await getDocumentDimensions(summaryPage);
462 |     // Use the tight bounding rect of the body's last child to avoid whitespace
463 |     // from the viewport height inflating scrollHeight/offsetHeight.
464 |     const summaryContentHeight = await summaryPage.evaluate(() => {
465 |       const body = document.body;
466 |       if (!body || !body.lastElementChild) return body ? body.scrollHeight : 0;
467 |       const rect = body.lastElementChild.getBoundingClientRect();
468 |       return Math.ceil(rect.bottom + (parseFloat(getComputedStyle(body).paddingBottom) || 0));
469 |     });
470 |     const summaryHeight = Math.max(summaryContentHeight + 20, 60);
471 |     const pdf3Buffer = await summaryPage.pdf({
472 |       width: `${Math.max(summaryDimensions.width + 20, widthValue)}px`,
473 |       height: `${summaryHeight}px`,
474 |       printBackground: true,
475 |       scale: 1,
476 |       margin: { top: '0px', right: '10px', bottom: '0px', left: '10px' },
477 |     });
478 |     await summaryPage.close();
479 | 
480 |     const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
481 |     const firstPdf = await PDFDocument.load(pdf1Buffer);
482 |     const secondPdf = await PDFDocument.load(pdf2Buffer);
483 |     const thirdPdf = await PDFDocument.load(pdf3Buffer);
484 | 
485 |     const [thirdPage] = await mergedPdf.copyPages(thirdPdf, [0]);
486 |     const [firstPdfPage] = await mergedPdf.copyPages(firstPdf, [0]);
487 |     const [secondPdfPage] = await mergedPdf.copyPages(secondPdf, [0]);
488 | 
489 |     mergedPdf.addPage(thirdPage);
490 |     mergedPdf.addPage(firstPdfPage);
491 | 
492 |     if (pdfMobileBuffer) {
493 |       const mobilePdf = await PDFDocument.load(pdfMobileBuffer);
494 |       const [mobilePdfPage] = await mergedPdf.copyPages(mobilePdf, [0]);
495 |       mergedPdf.addPage(mobilePdfPage);
496 |     }
497 | 
498 |     mergedPdf.addPage(secondPdfPage);
499 | 
500 |     mergedPdf.setTitle('Empower Engine');
501 |     mergedPdf.setAuthor('Arnab Adhikary');
502 |     mergedPdf.setSubject('Empower Engine');
503 |     mergedPdf.setKeywords(['pdf', 'metadata']);
504 |     mergedPdf.setProducer('Empower Engine');
505 |     mergedPdf.setCreator('PDF Maker Web');
506 |     mergedPdf.setCreationDate(new Date());
507 |     mergedPdf.setModificationDate(new Date());
508 | 
509 |     return Buffer.from(await mergedPdf.save());
510 |   } catch (error) {
511 |     console.error('Error generating PDF:', error);
512 |     throw error;
513 |   } finally {
514 |     await browser.close();
515 |   }
516 | }

 20 | function run(command, args) {
 21 |   const result = spawnSync(command, args, { encoding: "utf8", shell: false });
 22 |   if (result.error || result.status !== 0) return "";
 23 |   return (result.stdout || "").trim();

 60 | function readCachedExePath() {
 61 |   if (!exists(exeCachePath)) return "";

 64 |     if (cached && exists(cached)) return cached;

 67 | }

125 |     process.exit(1);
126 |   }

155 | function launchOneView({ attached = false } = {}) {
156 |   const oneViewExe = findOneViewExeFast() || findOneViewExe();

167 |

169 |     detached: !attached,

171 |     windowsHide: false,
172 |   });
173 | 
174 |   child.on("error", (err) => {
175 |     console.error("Failed to launch OneView:", err.message || err);
176 |     process.exit(1);
177 |   });
178 |

180 |   return child;
181 | }

 90 | function parseFilename(contentDispositionHeader) {
 91 |   if (!contentDispositionHeader) return null;
 92 |   const utf8Match = contentDispositionHeader.match(/filename\*=UTF-8''([^;]+)/i);
 93 |   if (utf8Match && utf8Match[1]) return decodeURIComponent(utf8Match[1]);
 94 |   const fallbackMatch = contentDispositionHeader.match(/filename="?([^"]+)"?/i);
 95 |   return fallbackMatch ? fallbackMatch[1] : null;
 96 | }
 97 | 
 98 | function downloadBlob(blob, fileName) {
 99 |   const blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
100 |   const anchor = document.createElement('a');
101 |   anchor.href = blobUrl;
102 |   anchor.download = fileName;
103 |   document.body.append(anchor);
104 |   anchor.click();
105 |   anchor.remove();
106 |   URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl);
107 | }
108 | 
109 | function setStatus(message, isError = false) {
110 |   status.textContent = message;
111 |   status.dataset.state = isError ? 'error' : 'ok';
112 | }
113 | 
114 | function setApiState(label, state) {
115 |   apiState.textContent = label;
116 |   apiState.dataset.state = state;
117 | }

119 | async function updateApiHealth() {
120 |   setApiState('Checking', 'pending');
121 | 
122 |   try {
123 |     const response = await fetch('/api/health');
124 |     if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Health check failed (${response.status})`);
125 | 
126 |     const responseBody = await response.json();
127 |     if (!responseBody.ok) throw new Error('API health endpoint returned not ok');
128 | 
129 |     setApiState('Online', 'ok');
130 |   } catch {
131 |     setApiState('Offline', 'error');
132 |   }
133 | }

161 |     });
162 |

164 |       let message = `Request failed with status ${response.status}`;
165 |       const contentType = response.headers.get('content-type') || '';
166 |       if (contentType.includes('application/json')) {
167 |         const errorBody = await response.json();
168 |         if (errorBody.message) message = errorBody.message;
169 |       } else {
170 |         const errorText = await response.text();
171 |         if (errorText) message = errorText;
172 |       }
173 |       throw new Error(message);
174 |     }
175 |

178 |     downloadBlob(pdfBlob, fileName);
179 |     setStatus(`PDF downloaded: ${fileName}`);
